In the past, you might have asked friends or family for recommendations, skimmed through your local phone book (remember the Yellow Pages?), or scanned newspaper articles for mentions of law firms. While these methods are still used today, they\u0026#8217;re not always the most efficient or reliable way to locate a good attorney.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIn today\u0026#8217;s digital age, many people turn to the internet, conducting online searches or sifting through multiple review websites to find a lawyer. These methods, while generally more accessible, might not always yield reliable results. Plus, they can be time-consuming and potentially costly.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eOne method that has stood the test of time in locating legal counsel is the \u003ca href=\"https://www.legalmatch.com/law-library/article/attorney-referral-services-in-california.html\"\u003eattorney referral service\u003c/a\u003e. This guide will dive into what attorney referral services are, how they work, and compare them with modern alternatives like LegalMatch to help you make an informed decision.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"js-table-of-contents\"\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003ch3 class=\"js-table-of-contents-target\"\u003eAttorney Referral Services: What Are They?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAttorney referral services are resources designed to connect people with lawyers who practice in the appropriate legal field for their cases. The Bar Association of a particular state typically organizes these services. In larger states, city or county bar associations may further categorize these services.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eFor instance, \u003ca href=\"https://www.legalmatch.com/law-library/article/attorney-referral-services-in-oklahoma.html\"\u003eif you\u0026#8217;re in Oklahoma and need a lawyer\u003c/a\u003e, the Oklahoma Bar Association provides a limited directory, but it doesn\u0026#8217;t offer an attorney referral service. If you require such a service and are located within the right jurisdictions, you can visit the Tulsa County Bar Association\u0026#8217;s website, which does provide an attorney referral service.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eServices provided by state and local bar associations usually charge between $20 to $25 per attorney referral.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3 class=\"js-table-of-contents-target\"\u003eHow Does an Attorney Referral Service Work?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSo, how does this attorney referral service work? You start by locating and contacting the service. You\u0026#8217;ll then need to explain your legal issue to a representative of the attorney referral service.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBased on the information you provide, the representative will comb through their database of attorneys and supply you with the contact details of a lawyer from their roster. But here\u0026#8217;s the catch: How do you know that the lawyer you\u0026#8217;re referred to best fits your specific case and not just the next attorney available to take a case? The sad truth is there\u0026#8217;s no real way to tell.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIf you want a selection of lawyers to choose from or wish to know more about the attorney you\u0026#8217;ve been referred to \u0026#8211; such as their case success rate \u0026#8211; then an attorney referral service might not be the most efficient method to find the right lawyer for you.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThis is reminiscent of the issues associated with using the Yellow Pages to find a lawyer, where an ad or phone number doesn\u0026#8217;t provide enough information to evaluate the lawyer\u0026#8217;s services. Using the Yellow Pages, like attorney referral services, can be hit-or-miss and often time-consuming.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3 class=\"js-table-of-contents-target\"\u003eThe LegalMatch Platform: A Modern Solution\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eRecognizing the need for a more efficient and reliable method, LegalMatch developed a platform to revolutionize the traditional way of finding the right lawyer.
